  "content": "```rust\n//! Generic utilities commonly used across VisuTility Orchestrator.\n//!\n//! The abstractions in this module are intentionally framework-agnostic:\n//! they do not depend on any particular CV/ML crate and can therefore be\n//! shared by every layer (Ingress, Data-Ops, Feature-Ops, \u2026).\n//!\n//! All functions are `#[inline]` where it makes sense to do so, and\n//! significant branches are annotated with `#[cold]` to let the optimizer\n//! keep hot-paths small.\n\nuse std::{\n    fmt,\n    fs::File,\n    io::Read,\n    path::{Path, PathBuf},\n    sync::atomic::{AtomicUsize, Ordering},\n    time::{Duration, Instant},\n};\n\nuse anyhow::{anyhow, Context, Result};\nuse once_cell::sync::Lazy;\nuse parking_lot::RwLock;\nuse serde::de::DeserializeOwned;\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, instrument};\n\n// Re-export the experiment tracker abstraction\npub mod experiment_tracker;\n\n/// VisuTility's generic error type for utility-layer operations.\n///\n/// We prefer using [`anyhow::Error`] at the top-level application\n/// boundary to allow for heterogeneous sources, but within the\n/// utility layer we capture the most common failure categories so that\n/// callers can still pattern-match when they need to.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum UtilError {\n    #[error(\"I/O error: {0}\")]\n    Io(#[from] std::io::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"serialization error: {0}\")]\n    Serde(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"configuration not found at path `{0}`\")]\n    ConfigNotFound(PathBuf),\n\n    #[error(\"task failed: {0}\")]\n    TaskFailed(String),\n}\n\n/// Generic wrapper around an [`Instant`] which logs the elapsed time at\n/// **drop**.  The measurement is therefore *scoped*; as soon as the guard\n/// goes out of scope, latency is emitted through the `tracing` facade.\n///\n/// ```no_run\n/// use visu_tility_utils::ScopedTimer;\n/// let _g = ScopedTimer::new(\"heavy_initialisation\");\n/// // \u2026 some expensive code \u2026\n\u2014 guard drops here and we get a log line with\n//   the elapsed time\n/// ```\npub struct ScopedTimer<'a> {\n    started: Instant,\n    label: &'a str,\n}\n\nimpl<'a> ScopedTimer<'a> {\n    /// Begin measuring elapsed time for the supplied label.\n    #[inline]\n    pub fn new(label: &'a str) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            started: Instant::now(),\n            label,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Stop the timer and return the [`Duration`] since creation without\n    /// logging. This allows manual control when automatic logging at `drop`\n    /// is not desired.\n    #[inline]\n    pub fn stop(self) -> Duration {\n        Instant::now() - self.started\n    }\n}\n\nimpl<'a> Drop for ScopedTimer<'a> {\n    fn drop(&mut self) {\n        let elapsed = Instant::now() - self.started;\n        info!(\n            label = %self.label,\n            ms = %elapsed.as_millis(),\n            \"ScopedTimer finished\"\n        );\n        METRICS\n            .write()\n            .record_duration(self.label, elapsed.as_secs_f64());\n    }\n}\n\n/// Global metrics collector with *zero* external dependencies.  This is\n/// intentionally minimal because higher layers might choose to forward these\n/// numbers to Prometheus, StatsD, or another monitoring backend.\n///\n/// Internally it stores *exponential moving averages* so that it can be used\n/// in hot-paths without unbounded memory growth.\npub struct Metrics {\n    /// Moving average of durations (seconds) per label.\n    durations: std::collections::HashMap<String, f64>,\n    /// EWMA smoothing factor in `[0,1]`.\n    alpha: f64,\n}\n\nimpl Metrics {\n    fn new(alpha: f64) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            durations: std::collections::HashMap::new(),\n            alpha,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Record a latency sample under `label`.\n    pub fn record_duration(&mut self, label: impl Into<String>, secs: f64) {\n        let label = label.into();\n        let entry = self.durations.entry(label).or_insert(secs);\n        // EWMA: v_t = alpha * x_t + (1-alpha) * v_{t-1}\n        *entry = self.alpha * secs + (1.0 - self.alpha) * *entry;\n    }\n\n    /// Return the current EWMA for `label`, if any.\n    pub fn duration_avg(&self, label: &str) -> Option<f64> {\n        self.durations.get(label).copied()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Static metrics instance; tweak the smoothing factor as needed.\n/// We protect it with a *fair* RwLock to allow many concurrent readers.\nstatic METRICS: Lazy<RwLock<Metrics>> = Lazy::new(|| RwLock::new(Metrics::new(0.20)));\n\n/// Typed representation of the global **application config**.\n///\n/// This is intentionally limited to fields that the utility layer needs\n/// to know about; higher layers maintain their own extensions.\n///\n/// Because config files are versioned in the Model Registry, we include a\n/// `schema_version` field to prevent silent breakage when the expected\n/// structure changes.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct AppConfig {\n    pub schema_version: u16,\n    pub experiment_tracking_uri: Option<String>,\n    pub model_registry_uri: Option<String>,\n    pub default_retry: RetryConfig,\n    /// Additional arbitrary key/value flavour that can be stored alongside\n    /// the canonical config.  Can be abused for feature flags, etc.\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub user: std::collections::HashMap<String, serde_json::Value>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct RetryConfig {\n    pub max_attempts: usize,\n    pub backoff_millis: u64,\n}\n\nimpl Default for RetryConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            max_attempts: 3,\n            backoff_millis: 500,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Maximum size (bytes) that we allow a configuration file to have before\n/// we refuse to load it.  Protects against accidental loading of huge blobs.\nconst MAX_CONFIG_SIZE: usize = 256 * 1024; // 256 KiB\n\n/// Load and parse application configuration **once** at start-up.\n///\n/// The file format is auto-detected based on extension (`.yaml`/`.yml` or\n/// `.json`).  The resulting struct is cached in a global `Lazy`.\n///\n/// Example:\n/// ```no_run\n/// let cfg = visu_tility_utils::config();\n/// println!(\"Schema v{} loaded\", cfg.schema_version);\n/// ```\nfn read_config_from_disk(path: &Path) -> Result<AppConfig> {\n    if !path.exists() {\n        return Err(UtilError::ConfigNotFound(path.into()).into());\n    }\n\n    let mut file =\n        File::open(path).with_context(|| format!(\"opening configuration file `{}`\", path.display()))?;\n\n    let mut buf = Vec::new();\n    file.read_to_end(&mut buf)\n        .with_context(|| format!(\"reading configuration file `{}`\", path.display()))?;\n\n    if buf.len() > MAX_CONFIG_SIZE {\n        return Err(anyhow!(\n            \"configuration file `{}` larger than {} KiB\",\n            path.display(),\n            MAX_CONFIG_SIZE / 1024\n        ));\n    }\n\n    let cfg = match path.extension().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) {\n        Some(\"yaml\") | Some(\"yml\") => serde_yaml::from_slice(&buf)?,\n        Some(\"json\") => serde_json::from_slice(&buf)?,\n        other => {\n            return Err(anyhow!(\n                \"unsupported configuration extension {:?} for `{}`\",\n                other,\n                path.display()\n            ))\n        }\n    };\n\n    Ok(cfg)\n}\n\n/// Discover the config path in the following order:\n///\n/// 1. Explicit argument via `VISU_CONFIG` environment variable.\n/// 2. `${CWD}/visu_config.yaml`\n/// 3. `${CWD}/visu_config.json`\nfn auto_discover_config() -> Option<PathBuf> {\n    if let Ok(path) = std::env::var(\"VISU_CONFIG\") {\n        return Some(PathBuf::from(path));\n    }\n\n    const CANDIDATES: &[&str] = &[\"visu_config.yaml\", \"visu_config.yml\", \"visu_config.json\"];\n    for c in CANDIDATES {\n        let p = PathBuf::from(c);\n        if p.exists() {\n            return Some(p);\n        }\n    }\n    None\n}\n\n/// Global application configuration singleton.\nstatic CONFIG: Lazy<AppConfig> = Lazy::new(|| {\n    let path = auto_discover_config()\n        .unwrap_or_else(|| PathBuf::from(\"visu_config.yaml\")); // fallback for nicer error msg\n    match read_config_from_disk(&path) {\n        Ok(cfg) => {\n            info!(\n                file = %path.display(),\n                version = cfg.schema_version,\n                \"configuration file loaded\"\n            );\n            cfg\n        }\n        Err(e) => {\n            error!(\n                file = %path.display(),\n                error = %e,\n                \"failed to load configuration; using built-in defaults\"\n            );\n            // Fallback\n            AppConfig {\n                schema_version: 0,\n                experiment_tracking_uri: None,\n                model_registry_uri: None,\n                default_retry: RetryConfig::default(),\n                user: Default::default(),\n            }\n        }\n    }\n});\n\n/// Access the application-wide [`AppConfig`].\n#[inline]\npub fn config() -> &'static AppConfig {\n    &CONFIG\n}\n\n/// Generic exponential *back-off* / *retry* helper.\n///\n/// The provided closure is executed until it either succeeds or\n/// max_attempts have been reached.\n///\n/// Usage:\n/// ```ignore\n/// use visu_tility_utils::retry;\n///\n/// let result = retry(\n///     &config().default_retry,\n///     || {\n///         // call external dependency that might fail\n///         some_unstable_operation()\n///     });\n/// ```\npub fn retry<F, T, E>(cfg: &RetryConfig, mut f: F) -> Result<T, E>\nwhere\n    F: FnMut() -> Result<T, E>,\n{\n    let mut attempt = 0;\n    loop {\n        match f() {\n            Ok(v) => return Ok(v),\n            Err(e) if attempt + 1 == cfg.max_attempts => return Err(e),\n            Err(_e) => {\n                attempt += 1;\n                std::thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(cfg.backoff_millis));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Simple **ID generator** that hands out monotonically increasing\n/// identifiers from a global counter.\n///\n/// This is useful when datasets or intermediate artefacts need a\n/// transaction-like handle but heavyweight UUIDs are overkill.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\npub struct Id(u64);\n\n// global counter\nstatic COUNTER: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(1);\n\nimpl Id {\n    /// Allocate a fresh id.\n    #[inline]\n    pub fn fresh() -> Self {\n        let n = COUNTER.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);\n        Id(n as u64)\n    }\n\n    /// Return the underlying integer.\n    #[inline]\n    pub fn as_u64(self) -> u64 {\n        self.0\n    }\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Id {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        self.0.fmt(f)\n    }\n}\n\n/// **Observer pattern**: runtime event bus.\n//\n/// Very light-weight publisher/subscriber abstraction built on top of\n/// [`crossbeam_channel`].  Since layers of the Orchestrator run in\n/// different scheduling contexts we cannot rely on *any* runtime; a\n/// channel-based design has zero dependencies on async executors.\npub mod event_bus {\n    use super::*;\n    use crossbeam_channel::{unbounded, Receiver, Sender};\n\n    /// Event types that travel on the bus.  This enum grows over time as new\n    /// features make use of the bus; by keeping it located in a *utility*\n    /// crate we avoid circular dependencies.\n    #[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n    pub enum Event {\n        HyperparameterTuningStarted { experiment_id: Id },\n        HyperparameterTuningFinished { experiment_id: Id },\n        ModelRegistered {\n            name: String,\n            version: String,\n            metadata: std::collections::HashMap<String, String>,\n        },\n        ModelDriftDetected {\n            model: String,\n            magnitude: f32,\n            timestamp: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>,\n        },\n        Custom(String, serde_json::Value),\n    }\n\n    /// Handle required for publishing events.\n    #[derive(Clone)]\n    pub struct Publisher {\n        tx: Sender<Event>,\n    }\n\n    impl Publisher {\n        /// Publish an event; errors are logged but otherwise ignored since the\n        /// system should remain functional even when no-one is listening.\n        pub fn publish(&self, evt: Event) {\n            if let Err(e) = self.tx.send(evt.clone()) {\n                debug!(error = ?e, event = ?evt, \"failed to publish event\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// A stream of events.\n    pub type Subscription = Receiver<Event>;\n\n    /// Construct a **single** global bus so that layers can obtain\n    /// cheap clones of the `Publisher` without having to pass them around.\n    static BUS: Lazy<(Publisher, Subscription)> = Lazy::new(|| {\n        let (tx, rx) = unbounded::<Event>();\n        (Publisher { tx }, rx)\n    });\n\n    /// Return a handle for *publishing* events.\n    pub fn publisher() -> Publisher {\n        BUS.0.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Subscribe to events.  Every caller receives a *clone* of the receiver\n    /// which means all subscribers see *all* events (fan-out).\n    pub fn subscribe() -> Subscription {\n        BUS.1.clone()\n    }\n}\n\n/// A small proc-macro-like helper (implemented as declarative macro to avoid meta\n/// crate) for scoped timing.\n///\n/// ```\n/// visu_tility_utils::scope_time!(\"fancy_stage\", {\n///     expensive();\n/// });\n/// ```\n#[macro_export]\nmacro_rules! scope_time {\n    ($label:expr, $block:block) => {{\n        let _g = $crate::ScopedTimer::new($label);\n        $block\n    }};\n}\n\n/// Low-level metric client for experiment tracking.\n///\n/// This struct is crate-private and should only be accessed through the\n/// `ExperimentTracker` trait abstraction in the `experiment_tracker` module.\n/// It provides direct integration with the underlying metrics infrastructure.\npub(crate) struct RawMetricClient {\n    endpoint: String,\n}\n\nimpl RawMetricClient {\n    /// Create a new metric client pointing to the specified endpoint.\n    pub(crate) fn new(endpoint: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            endpoint: endpoint.into(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Log a scalar metric value at a given training step.\n    pub(crate) fn log_scalar(&self, metric_name: &str, value: f64, step: u64) {\n        info!(\n            endpoint = %self.endpoint,\n            metric = %metric_name,\n            value = %value,\n            step = %step,\n            \"RawMetricClient: logged scalar\"\n        );\n    }\n\n    /// Log a hyperparameter configuration.\n    pub(crate) fn log_hyperparameter(&self, param_name: &str, value: &str) {\n        info!(\n            endpoint = %self.endpoint,\n            param = %param_name,\n            value = %value,\n            \"RawMetricClient: logged hyperparameter\"\n        );\n    }\n\n    /// Upload a model artifact to the tracking server.\n    pub(crate) fn upload_model_artifact(\n        &self,\n }\n}\n\n/// Tests live inside the same file so that the utils crate remains\n/// a **single** compilation unit. integer.\n    #[inline]\n    pub fn as_u64(self) -> u64 {\n        self.0\n    }\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Id {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        self.0.fmt(f)\n    }\n}\n\n/// **Observer pattern**: runtime event bus.\n//\n/// Very light-weight publisher/subscriber abstraction built on top of\n/// [`crossbeam_channel`]. Every caller receives a *clone* of the receiver\n    /// which means all subscribers see *all* events (fan-out).\n    pub fn subscribe() -> Subscription {\n        BUS.1.clone()\n    }\n}\n\n/// A  pub fn new(buffer: usize) -> Self {\n        let (tx, _) = broadcast::channel(buffer);\n        Self { tx }\n    }\n\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> broadcast::Receiver<TuningEvent> {\n        self.tx.subscribe()\n    }\n\n    pub fn emit(&self, e: TuningEvent) {\n        // Ignoring send errors (occurs if no receiver is listening).\n        let _ = self.tx.send(e);\n    }\n}\n\n/// Trait self.context.event_bus.clone()\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl<T> HyperParamTuner for RandomSearchTuner<T>\nwhere\n    T: ModelTrainer + 'static,\n{\n    #[instrument(skip_all, name = &TuningEventBus,\n    observer: Arc<O>,\n) -> tokio::task::JoinHandle<()> {\n    let mut rx = bus.subscribe();\n    tokio::spawn(async move {\n        while let Ok(event) = rx.recv().await {\n            match event {\n                TuningEvent::TrialStart { trial_id, params } => {\n                    observer.on_trial_start(trial_id, &params).await;\n                }\n .on_trial_complete(trial_id, &params, &metric)\n                        .await;\n                }\n                TuningEvent::TuningComplete { result } => {\n                    observer.on_tuning_complete(&result).await;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    })\n}\n\n/// Log hyperparameters using the ExperimentTracker trait abstraction.\n///\n/// This function This module glues together three critical concerns of the VisuTility\n//! Orchestrator platform:\n//!\n//! 1. Strategy Pattern\u2010based hyper-parameter tuning\n//! 2. Observer Pattern\u2010based model monitoring\n//! 3. Automated retraining triggers\n//!\n//! The code is completely self-contained and can be compiled and unit-tested\n//! in isolation.  In the full platform the public interfaces defined here\n//! are re-exported by the *Model Ops* layer.\n//!\n//! This module uses the `ExperimentTracker` trait abstraction for all\n//! experiment tracking operations, enabling easy swapping of backends\n//! and mock-based testing.\n//!\n//! Dependencies\n//! ------------\n//! The following third-party crates are required in `Cargo.toml`.\n//!\n//! ```toml\n//! [dependencies]\n//! async-trait = \"0.1\"\n//! rand        = \"0.8\"\n//! thiserror   = \"1.0\"\n//! tokio       = { version = \"1\", features = [\"full\"] }\n//! log         = \"0.4\"\n//! ```\n//!\n//! Note: In production, all blocking\u2010IO should be pushed to separate worker\n//! pools; here tokio is used for concise asynchronous examples.\n\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse std::path::Path;\nuse std::sync::{Arc, RwLock};\nuse std::time::{Duration, SystemTime};\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse log::{debug, error, info, warn};\nuse rand::distributions::{Distribution, Uniform};\nuse rand::rngs::ThreadRng;\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::task;\nuse tokio::time::sleep;\n\nuse crate::experiment_tracker::ExperimentTracker;\n\n//\n// Domain Types\n// ------------\n\n/// A unique model identifier.\npub type ModelId = String;\n\n/// A simplistic representation of metric values keyed by their names.\npub type Metrics = HashMap<String, f64>;\n\n/// Hyper-parameter key/value store.  A real implementation would likely use\n/// strongly-typed parameters and ranges.\npub type HyperParams = HashMap<String, f64>;\n\n/// Raw training data handle.  In production this would wrap an Arrow table,\n/// Parquet reader, or a stream of image tensors.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct DataBatch {\n    pub num_samples: usize,\n}\n\n//\n// Error Handling\n// --------------\n\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum ModelOpsError {\n    #[error(\"model `{0}` not found\")]\n    ModelNotFound(ModelId),\n\n    #[error(\"failed to spawn background task: {0}\")]\n    TaskSpawnError(String),\n\n    #[error(\"training failed: {0}\")]\n    TrainingFailed(String),\n\n    #[error(\"registry error: {0}\")]\n    Registry(String),\n}\n\n//\n//  Model Registry\n// ---------------\n\n/// Metadata for a single, immutable model version.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ModelVersion {\n    pub version: u64,\n    pub trained_at: SystemTime,\n    pub hyper_params: HyperParams,\n    pub metrics: Metrics,\n}\n\n/// Thread-safe, in-memory implementation of a model registry.\n///\n/// In production this would be backed by a SQL/NoSQL database with audit\n/// logging. All writes are versioned and immutable.\n#[derive(Debug, Default, Clone)]\npub struct ModelRegistry {\n    inner: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<ModelId, Vec<ModelVersion>>>>,\n}\n\nimpl ModelRegistry {\n    /// Registers a new model version and returns the assigned version number.\n    pub fn register(\n        &self,\n        id: &ModelId,\n        hyper_params: HyperParams,\n        metrics: Metrics,\n    ) -> Result<u64, ModelOpsError> {\n        let mut guard = self\n            .inner\n            .write()\n            .map_err(|e| ModelOpsError::Registry(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        let versions = guard.entry(id.clone()).or_default();\n        let version_num = versions\n            .last()\n            .map(|v| v.version + 1)\n            .unwrap_or(1);\n\n        versions.push(ModelVersion {\n            version: version_num,\n            trained_at: SystemTime::now(),\n            hyper_params,\n            metrics,\n        });\n\n        info!(\"Registered model `{id}` version {version_num}\");\n        Ok(version_num)\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the latest model version.\n    pub fn latest(&self, id: &ModelId) -> Result<ModelVersion, ModelOpsError> {\n        let guard = self\n            .inner\n            .read()\n            .map_err(|e| ModelOpsError::Registry(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        guard\n            .get(id)\n            .and_then(|v| v.last().cloned())\n            .ok_or_else(|| ModelOpsError::ModelNotFound(id.clone()))\n    }\n}\n\n//\n// Strategy Pattern: Hyper-Parameter Tuners\n// ---------------------------------------\n\n/// Strategies must implement asynchronous tuning given a model id and data.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait HyperParamTuner: Send + Sync {\n    async fn tune(\n        &self,\n        model_id: &ModelId,\n        data: &DataBatch,\n    ) -> Result<HyperParams, ModelOpsError>;\n}\n\n/// A simple grid search tuner.\npub struct GridSearchTuner {\n    learning_rates: Vec<f64>,\n    num_layers: Vec<f64>,\n}\n\nimpl GridSearchTuner {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            learning_rates: vec![1e-4, 1e-3, 1e-2],\n            num_layers: vec![2.0, 3.0, 4.0],\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl HyperParamTuner for GridSearchTuner {\n    async fn tune(\n        &self,\n        model_id: &ModelId,\n        data: &DataBatch,\n    ) -> Result<HyperParams, ModelOpsError> {\n        info!(\n            \"Running grid search for model `{}` on {} samples\",\n            model_id, data.num_samples\n        );\n\n        // Dummy evaluation metric: random value \u2208 [0,1]\n        let mut best_metric = f64::MIN;\n        let mut best_params = HyperParams::new();\n\n        for lr in &self.learning_rates {\n            for layers in &self.num_layers {\n                let simulated_metric = 1.0 / (lr * layers); // deterministic but arbitrary\n                if simulated_metric > best_metric {\n                    best_metric = simulated_metric;\n                    best_params.insert(\"learning_rate\".into(), *lr);\n                    best_params.insert(\"num_layers\".into(), *layers);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Grid search selected params: {:?}\", best_params);\n        Ok(best_params)\n    }\n}\n\n/// A random search tuner.\npub struct RandomSearchTuner {\n    trials: usize,\n    rng: ThreadRng,\n}\n\nimpl RandomSearchTuner {\n    pub fn new(trials: usize) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            trials,\n            rng: rand::thread_rng(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl HyperParamTuner for RandomSearchTuner {\n    async fn tune(\n        &self,\n        model_id: &ModelId,\n        data: &DataBatch,\n    ) -> Result<HyperParams, ModelOpsError> {\n        info!(\n            \"Running random search for model `{}` with {} trials\",\n            model_id, self.trials\n        );\n\n        let lr_dist = Uniform::new(1e-4, 1e-2);\n        let layer_dist = Uniform::new_inclusive(2.0, 6.0);\n\n        let mut best_metric = f64::MIN;\n        let mut best_params = HyperParams::new();\n\n        for _ in 0..self.trials {\n            let lr = lr_dist.sample(&mut self.rng);\n            let layers = layer_dist.sample(&mut self.rng);\n            let simulated_metric = 1.0 / (lr * layers);\n\n            if simulated_metric > best_metric {\n                best_metric = simulated_metric;\n                best_params.insert(\"learning_rate\".into(), lr);\n                best_params.insert(\"num_layers\".into(), layers);\n            }\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Random search selected params: {:?}\", best_params);\n        Ok(best_params)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Factory for obtaining the right tuner based on contextual information.\n///\n/// In production this might inspect the model type, data modality, or\n/// tenancy metadata.\npub enum TunerKind {\n    GridSearch,\n    RandomSearch { trials: usize },\n}\n\npub fn tuner_factory(kind: TunerKind) -> Arc<dyn HyperParamTuner> {\n    match kind {\n        TunerKind::GridSearch => Arc::new(GridSearchTuner::new()),\n        TunerKind::RandomSearch { trials } => Arc::new(RandomSearchTuner::new(trials)),\n    }\n}\n\n//\n// Observer Pattern: Metrics Events & Subscriptions\n// -----------------------------------------------\n\n/// A metrics event emitted by the serving layer.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MetricsEvent {\n    pub model_id: ModelId,\n    pub metrics: Metrics,\n}\n\n/// Observer trait used by any consumer interested in metrics events.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait Observer: Send + Sync {\n    async fn update(&self, event: MetricsEvent);\n}\n\n/// Subject trait implemented by event producers.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait Subject {\n    async fn add_observer(&self, observer: Arc<dyn Observer>);\n    async fn notify(&self, event: MetricsEvent);\n}\n\n/// Model monitor aggregates runtime metrics and notifies observers when\n/// degradation is detected.\n#[derive(Default)]\npub struct ModelMonitor {\n    observers: Arc<RwLock<Vec<Arc<dyn Observer>>>>,\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl Subject for ModelMonitor {\n    async fn add_observer(&self, observer: Arc<dyn Observer>) {\n        let mut guard = self\n            .observers\n            .write()\n            .expect(\"poisoned lock in ModelMonitor\");\n        guard.push(observer);\n    }\n\n    async fn notify(&self, event: MetricsEvent) {\n        debug!(\"Notifying {} observers\", self.observers.read().unwrap().len());\n        for obs in self.observers.read().unwrap().iter() {\n            obs.update(event.clone()).await;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n//\n// Experiment Tracking Integration\n// -------------------------------\n\n/// Log hyperparameters to an experiment tracker.\n///\n/// This function accepts any type that implements the `ExperimentTracker` trait,\n/// allowing for easy testing with mocks and swapping of tracking backends.\npub fn log_hyperparams<T: ExperimentTracker>(\n    tracker: &T,\n    params: &HyperParams,\n) {\n    for (name, value) in params {\n        tracker.log_hyperparameter(name, &value.to_string());\n    }\n}\n\n/// Log training metrics to an experiment tracker.\n///\n/// Records each metric in the provided map at the specified step.\npub fn log_training_metrics<T: ExperimentTracker>(\n    tracker: &T,\n    metrics: &Metrics,\n    step: u64,\n) {\n    for (name, value) in metrics {\n        tracker.log_scalar(name, *value, step);\n    }\n}\n\n/// Upload a model artifact using the experiment tracker.\n///\n/// Delegates to the tracker's `upload_model_artifact` method.\npub fn remote_name)\n}\n\n//\n// Automated Retrainer\n// -------------------\n\n/// Retrains a model when metrics fall below a dynamic threshold.\npub struct AutoRetrainer<T: ExperimentTracker + 'static> {\n In production this would call into a training\n    /// service, ship GPU jobs, etc.\n    async fn train_model(\n        &self,\n        model_id: &ModelId,\n        hyper_params: HyperParams,\n        data: DataBatch,\n    ) -> Result<Metrics, ModelOpsError> {\n        info!(\"Training model `{model_id}` with params {:?}\", hyper_params);\n\n        // Log hyperparameters to tracker\n        log_hyperparams(self.tracker.as_ref(), &hyper_params);\n\n        // Fake training latency\n        sleep(Duration::from_millis(500)).await;\n\n        // Return fake metrics inversely proportional to learning rate\n        let val_accuracy = 0.85\n            + 0.1 * (1e-2 - hyper_params[\"learning_rate\"]).clamp(0.0, 1e-2) / 1e-2;\n\n        let metrics = HashMap::from([(\"val_accuracy\".into(), val_accuracy)]);\n\n        // Log training metrics\n        log_training_metrics(self.tracker.as_ref(), &metrics, 1);\n\n        Ok(metrics)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run a complete training pipeline with ExperimentTracker>(\n    tracker: &T,\n    tuner: Arc<dyn HyperParamTuner>,\n    model_id: &ModelId,\n    data: DataBatch,\n    registry: &ModelRegistry,\n) -> Result<u64, ModelOpsError> {\n    // val_accuracy)]);\n\n    // Step 3: Log metrics\n    log_training_metrics(tracker, &metrics, 1);\n\n    // Step 4: Register model\n    let version = registry.register(model_id, params, metrics)?;\n\n    info!(\"Model `{model_id}` trained and registered as version {version}\");\n    Ok(version)\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl<T: ExperimentTracker + Send + Sync + 'static> Observer for AutoRetrainer<T> {\n    async fn update(&self, event: MetricsEvent) {\n        let acc = event.metrics.get(\"val_accuracy\").cloned().unwrap_or(1.0);\n        if acc >= self.degradation_threshold {\n            debug!(\n                \"Model `{}` accuracy {:.3} above threshold {:.3}, no action.\",\n                event.model_id, acc, self.degradation_threshold\n            );\n            return;\n        }\n\n };\n\n            // Step 2: Hyper-parameter tuning\n            let tuned_params = tuner_clone.tune(&model_id, &data).await?;\n\n            // Log hyperparameters using the tracker\n tuned_params.clone(),\n                data,\n                tracker_clone.as_ref(),\n            ).await?;\n\n            // Step 4: Register new version\n            registry_clone\n                .register(&model_id, tuned_params, new_metrics)\n                .map(|v| info!(\"Model `{}` retrained, new version {}\", model_id, v))\n        })\n        .await\n        {\n            error!(\"Failed to spawn retraining task: {e}\");\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// A static helper so we can move it into the spawned async task easily.\nasync fn train_model_static<T: ExperimentTracker>(\n    model_id: &ModelId,\n    hyper_params: HyperParams,\n    _data: DataBatch,\n    tracker: &T,\n) -> Result<Metrics, ModelOpsError> {\n    info!(\"Training model `{model_id}` HashMap::from([(\"val_accuracy\".into(), val_accuracy)]);\n\n    // Log training metrics\n    log_training_metrics(tracker, &metrics, 1);\n\n    Ok(metrics)\n}\n\n//\n// Example Usage\n// -------------\n//! Compile via `cargo run --features demo`.\n#[cfg(feature = \"demo\")]\n#[tokio::main]\nasync fn main() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n    use 0.92, // Threshold\n        Arc::clone(&tracker),\n    ));\n    monitor.add_observer(retrainer).await;\n\n    // Emit some events \u2013 normally this comes from the serving layer.\n    let events = This module glues together three critical concerns of the VisuTility\n//! Orchestrator platform:\n//!\n//! 1. Strategy Pattern\u2010based hyper-parameter tuning\n//! 2. In the full platform the public interfaces defined here\n//! are re-exported by the *Model Ops* layer.\n//!\n//! This module uses the `ExperimentTracker` trait abstraction for all\n//! experiment tracking operations, enabling easy swapping of backends\n//! and mock-based testing.\n//!\n//! Dependencies\n//! ------------\n//! The following third-party crates are required in `Cargo.toml`.\n//!\n//! ```toml\n//! [dependencies]\n//! async-trait = \"0.1\"\n//! rand        = \"0.8\"\n//! thiserror   = \"1.0\"\n//! tokio       = { version = \"1\", features = [\"full\"] }\n//! log         = \"0.4\"\n//! ```\n//!\n//! Note: In production, all blocking\u2010IO should be pushed to separate worker\n//! pools; here tokio is used for concise asynchronous examples.\n\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse std::path::Path;\nuse std::sync::{Arc, RwLock};\nuse std::time::{Duration, SystemTime};\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse log::{debug, error, info, warn};\nuse rand::distributions::{Distribution, Uniform};\nuse rand::rngs::ThreadRng;\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::task;\nuse tokio::time::sleep;\n\nuse crate::experiment_tracker::ExperimentTracker;\n\n//\n// Domain Types\n// ------------\n\n/// A unique model identifier.\npub type ModelId = String;\n\n/// A simplistic representation of metric values keyed by their names.\npub type Metrics = HashMap<String, f64>;\n\n/// Hyper-parameter key/value store.  A real implementation would likely use\n/// strongly-typed parameters and ranges.\npub type HyperParams = HashMap<String, f64>;\n\n/// Raw training data handle.  In production this would wrap an Arrow table,\n/// Parquet reader, or a stream of image tensors.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct DataBatch {\n    pub num_samples: usize,\n}\n\n//\n// Error Handling\n// --------------\n\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum ModelOpsError {\n    #[error(\"model `{0}` not found\")]\n    ModelNotFound(ModelId),\n\n    #[error(\"failed to spawn background task: {0}\")]\n    TaskSpawnError(String),\n\n    #[error(\"training failed: {0}\")]\n    TrainingFailed(String),\n\n    #[error(\"registry error: {0}\")]\n    Registry(String),\n}\n\n//\n//  Model Registry\n// ---------------\n\n/// Metadata for a single, immutable model version.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ModelVersion {\n    pub version: u64,\n    pub trained_at: SystemTime,\n    pub hyper_params: HyperParams,\n    pub metrics: Metrics,\n}\n\n/// Thread-safe, in-memory implementation of a model registry.\n///\n/// In production this would be backed by a SQL/NoSQL database with audit\n/// logging. All writes are versioned and immutable.\n#[derive(Debug, Default, Clone)]\npub struct ModelRegistry {\n    inner: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<ModelId, Vec<ModelVersion>>>>,\n}\n\nimpl ModelRegistry {\n    /// Registers a new model version and returns the assigned version number.\n    pub fn register(\n        &self,\n        id: &ModelId,\n        hyper_params: HyperParams,\n        metrics: Metrics,\n    ) -> Result<u64, ModelOpsError> {\n        let mut guard = self\n            .inner\n            .write()\n            .map_err(|e| ModelOpsError::Registry(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        let versions = guard.entry(id.clone()).or_default();\n        let version_num = versions\n            .last()\n            .map(|v| v.version + 1)\n            .unwrap_or(1);\n\n        versions.push(ModelVersion {\n            version: version_num,\n            trained_at: SystemTime::now(),\n            hyper_params,\n            metrics,\n        });\n\n        info!(\"Registered model `{id}` version {version_num}\");\n        Ok(version_num)\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the latest model version.\n    pub fn latest(&self, id: &ModelId) -> Result<ModelVersion, ModelOpsError> {\n        let guard = self\n            .inner\n            .read()\n            .map_err(|e| ModelOpsError::Registry(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        guard\n            .get(id)\n            .and_then(|v| v.last().cloned())\n            .ok_or_else(|| ModelOpsError::ModelNotFound(id.clone()))\n    }\n}\n\n//\n// Strategy Pattern: Hyper-Parameter Tuners\n// ---------------------------------------\n\n/// Strategies must implement asynchronous tuning given a model id and data.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait HyperParamTuner: Send + Sync {\n    async fn tune(\n        &self,\n        model_id: &ModelId,\n        data: &DataBatch,\n    ) -> Result<HyperParams, ModelOpsError>;\n}\n\n/// A simple grid search tuner.\npub struct GridSearchTuner {\n    learning_rates: Vec<f64>,\n    num_layers: Vec<f64>,\n}\n\nimpl GridSearchTuner {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            learning_rates: vec![1e-4, 1e-3, 1e-2],\n            num_layers: vec![2.0, 3.0, 4.0],\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl HyperParamTuner for GridSearchTuner {\n    async fn tune(\n        &self,\n        model_id: &ModelId,\n        data: &DataBatch,\n    ) -> Result<HyperParams, ModelOpsError> {\n        info!(\n            \"Running grid search for model `{}` on {} samples\",\n            model_id, data.num_samples\n        );\n\n        // Dummy evaluation metric: random value \u2208 [0,1]\n        let mut best_metric = f64::MIN;\n        let mut best_params = HyperParams::new();\n\n        for lr in &self.learning_rates {\n            for layers in &self.num_layers {\n                let simulated_metric = 1.0 / (lr * layers); // deterministic but arbitrary\n                if simulated_metric > best_metric {\n                    best_metric = simulated_metric;\n                    best_params.insert(\"learning_rate\".into(), *lr);\n                    best_params.insert(\"num_layers\".into(), *layers);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Grid search selected params: {:?}\", best_params);\n        Ok(best_params)\n    }\n}\n\n/// A random search tuner.\npub struct RandomSearchTuner {\n    trials: usize,\n }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl HyperParamTuner for RandomSearchTuner {\n    async fn tune(\n        &self,\n        model_id: &ModelId,\n        data: &DataBatch,\n    ) -> Result<HyperParams, ModelOpsError> {\n        info!(\n            \"Running random search for model `{}` with {} trials\",\n            model_id, self.trials\n        );\n\n        let lr_dist = Uniform::new(1e-4, 1e-2);\n        let layer_dist = Uniform::new_inclusive(2.0, 6.0);\n\n        let mut best_metric = f64::MIN;\n        let mut best_params = HyperParams::new();\n\n        for _ in 0..self.trials {\n            let lr = lr_dist.sample(&mut self.rng);\n            let layers = layer_dist.sample(&mut self.rng);\n            let simulated_metric = 1.0 / (lr * layers);\n\n            if simulated_metric > best_metric {\n                best_metric = simulated_metric;\n                best_params.insert(\"learning_rate\".into(), lr);\n                best_params.insert(\"num_layers\".into(), layers);\n            }\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Random search selected params: {:?}\", best_params);\n        Ok(best_params)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Factory GridSearch,\n    RandomSearch { trials: usize },\n}\n\npub fn tuner_factory(kind: TunerKind) -> Arc<dyn HyperParamTuner> {\n    match kind {\n        TunerKind::GridSearch => -----------------------------------------------\n\n/// A metrics event emitted by the serving layer.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MetricsEvent {\n    pub model_id: ModelId,\n    pub metrics: Subject trait implemented by event producers.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait Subject {\n    async fn add_observer(&self, observer: Arc<dyn Observer>);\n    async fn notify(&self, event: .observers\n            .write()\n            .expect(\"poisoned lock in ModelMonitor\");\n        guard.push(observer);\n    }\n\n    async fn notify(&self, event: MetricsEvent) {\n        debug!(\"Notifying {} observers\", self.observers.read().unwrap().len());\n        for obs in self.observers.read().unwrap().iter() {\n            obs.update(event.clone()).await;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n//\n// Experiment Tracking Integration\n// -------------------------------\n\n/// Log hyperparameters to an experiment tracker.\n///\n/// This function accepts any type that implements the   async fn update(&self, event: MetricsEvent) {\n        let acc = event.metrics.get(\"val_accuracy\").cloned().unwrap_or(1.0);\n        if acc >= self.degradation_threshold {\n            debug!(\n This module wires together the Strategy + Observer patterns to:\n//!   1. Collect model-serving metrics from asynchronous sources\n//!   2. Detect drift / SLA violations through pluggable observers\n//!   3. Decide\u2014via retraining strategy\u2014whether automated retraining should start\n//!   4. Emit retraining jobs into an async work-queue for downstream processing\n//!\n//! The implementation is intentionally self-contained so it can be compiled\n//! standalone for unit-testing, yet is ready to be integrated into the wider\n//! `VisuTility Orchestrator` platform.\n//!\n//! This module uses the `ExperimentTracker` trait abstraction for experiment\n//! tracking, instantiating `DefaultTracker` for production use.\n//!\n//! External crates used:\n//!   - tokio      (async runtime + channels)\n//!   - anyhow     (error propagation)\n//!   - serde      (de/serialization of metric payloads)\n//!   - thiserror  (typed error   #[error(\"metrics channel closed\")]\n    ChannelClosed,\n    #[error(\"failed to send retraining job: {0}\")]\n    RetrainSend(String),\n    #[error(\"internal error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n}\n\n/// Public handle that can be cloned and used by inference workers to\n/// asynchronously submit new metric events.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct MetricSink {\n    tx:     .map_err(|_| MonitorError::ChannelClosed)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Public stream (subscriber) receiving retraining jobs that need handling\n/// downstream by Model-Ops components (e.g. a trainer accuracy: Option<f64>,\n    ) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            model_id: model_id.into(),\n            ts: SystemTime::now()\n                .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)\n                .expect(\"time went backwards\")\n                .as_millis(),\n            latency_ms,\n            throughput,\n            accuracy,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Rolling collection of metric events for a single model.\n#[derive(Debug, Default)]\nstruct MetricWindow {\n    /// Time-ordered ring-buffer\n    events: VecDeque<MetricEvent>,\n    /// Pre-aggregated stats for constant-time self.events.len() == MAX_WINDOW_SIZE {\n            if let Some(old) = self.events.pop_front() {\n                self.latency_sum -= old.latency_ms;\n                self.throughput_sum -= old.throughput;\n                if let Some(acc) = old.accuracy {\n                    self.accuracy_sum -= acc;\n                    self.accuracy_cnt -= 1;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        self.latency_sum += evt.latency_ms;\n        self.throughput_sum += evt.throughput;\n        if let Some(acc) = evt.accuracy {\n            self.accuracy_sum += acc;\n            self.accuracy_cnt += 1;\n        }\n\n        self.events.push_back(evt);\n    }\n\n    fn len(&self) -> usize {\n        self.events.len()\n    }\n\n    fn mean_latency(&self) -> f64 {\n        if self.events.is_empty() {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n        self.latency_sum / self.events.len() as f64\n    }\n\n    fn mean_throughput(&self) -> f64 {\n        if self.events.is_empty() {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n        self.throughput_sum / self.events.len() as f64\n    }\n\n    fn mean_accuracy(&self) -> Option<f64> {\n        if self.accuracy_cnt == 0 {\n            None\n        } else {\n            Some(self.accuracy_sum / self.accuracy_cnt as f64)\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn p99_latency(&self) -> f64 {\n        // naive percentile calc (production code may use histogram)\n        if self.events.is_empty() {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n        let mut latencies: Vec<_> = self.events.iter().map(|e| e.latency_ms).collect();\n        latencies.sort_by(|a, b| a.partial_cmp(b).unwrap());\n        let idx = ((latencies.len() as f64) * 0.99).ceil() as usize - 1;\n        latencies[idx]\n    }\n}\n\n/// What action an Observer suggests.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq)]\nenum MonitorAction {\n    Noop,\n    FlagRetrain,\n}\n\n/// Observer Pattern: notified of each model's aggregated metrics.\ntrait MetricObserver: Send + Sync {\n    /// Name (for logging/metrics)\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str;\n    /// Evaluate window; return action.\n    fn on_update(&self, model: &str, window: &MetricWindow) -> MonitorAction;\n}\n\n/// Observer that triggers retraining when P99 latency > threshold.\nstruct LatencySlaObserver {\n    /// milliseconds\n    threshold_ms: f64,\n}\n\nimpl LatencySlaObserver {\n    fn new(threshold_ms: f64) -> Self {\n        Self { threshold_ms }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MetricObserver for LatencySlaObserver {\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"latency_sla\"\n    }\n\n    fn on_update(&self, model: &str, window: &MetricWindow) -> MonitorAction {\n        let p99 = window.p99_latency();\n        gauge!(\"model.p99_latency\", p99, \"model\" => model);\n        if p99 > self.threshold_ms {\n            warn!(\n                \"Model {} P99 latency {:.2}ms above threshold {:.2}ms\",\n                model, p99, self.threshold_ms\n            );\n            return MonitorAction::FlagRetrain;\n        }\n        MonitorAction::Noop\n    }\n}\n\n/// Observer that detects accuracy drift below threshold.\nstruct AccuracyDriftObserver {\n    min_accuracy: f64,\n}\n\nimpl AccuracyDriftObserver {\n    fn new(min_accuracy: f64) -> Self {\n        Self { min_accuracy }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MetricObserver for AccuracyDriftObserver {\n    fn name(&self) -> gauge!(\"model.accuracy\", acc, \"model\" => model);\n            if acc < self.min_accuracy {\n                warn!(\n                    \"Model {} accuracy {:.4} below threshold {:.4}\",\n                    model, acc, self.min_accuracy\n                );\n                return MonitorAction::FlagRetrain;\n            }\n        }\n        MonitorAction::Noop\n    }\n}\n\n/// An internal representation of a retraining job request.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct RetrainJob {\n    pub model_id: String,\n    pub reason: String,\n    pub requested_at: /// Called periodically with aggregated observer actions\n    async fn evaluate(\n        &self,\n        model: &str,\n        actions: &[MonitorAction],\n        window: &MetricWindow,\n    ) -> Option<RetrainJob>;\n}\n\n/// Simple majority-vote strategy: if any FlagRetrain action is present,\n/// we create a job. Implements a debounce window to avoid spamming.\nstruct MajorityStrategy {\n    /// minimum time between two jobs for the same model\n    cooldown: Duration,\n    /// book-keeping of last job timestamps\n    last_job_ts: Arc<RwLock<dashmap::DashMap<String, u128>>>,\n}\n\nimpl MajorityStrategy {\n    fn new(cooldown: Duration) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            cooldown,\n            last_job_ts: Arc::new(RwLock::new(dashmap::DashMap::new())),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\nimpl RetrainStrategy for MajorityStrategy {\n    async fn evaluate(\n        &self,\n        model: &str,\n        actions: &[MonitorAction],\n        _window: &MetricWindow,\n    ) -> Option<RetrainJob> {\n        if !actions.iter().any(|a| *a == MonitorAction::FlagRetrain) {\n            return None;\n        }\n\n        let now = SystemTime::now()\n            .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)\n            .unwrap()\n            .as_millis();\n\n        {\n            let m = self.last_job_ts.read().await;\n            if let Some(entry) = m.get(model) {\n                let last = *entry;\n                if now - last < self.cooldown.as_millis() {\n                    debug!(\"Skipping retrain for {model} due to cooldown\");\n                    return None;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        {\n            let mut m = self.last_job_ts.write().await;\n            m.insert(model.to_string(), now);\n        }\n\n        Some(RetrainJob {\n            model_id: model.to_string(),\n            reason: \"observer_trigger\".into(),\n            requested_at: now,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Create a DefaultTracker instance for experiment tracking.\n///\n/// This function creates the production tracker that wraps the internal\n/// `RawMetricClient`. endpoint.unwrap_or(DEFAULT_TRACKING_ENDPOINT);\n    DefaultTracker::new(tracking_endpoint)\n}\n\n/// Central engine wiring together observers + strategy.\npub struct MonitorEngine<T: ExperimentTracker + Send + Sync + 'static> {\n    metric_sink: MetricSink,\n    retrain_job_stream: RetrainJobStream,\n    /// keep JoinHandles for graceful shutdown\n    tasks: Vec<JoinHandle<()>>,\n    /// Experiment {\n    /// Start a new MonitorEngine with a custom tracker implementation.\n    ///\n    /// This allows for dependency injection of different tracker implementations,\n    /// including mocks for testing.\n    pub fn start_with_tracker(\n        observers: Vec<Box<dyn MetricObserver>>,\n        strategy: Arc<dyn RetrainStrategy>,\n        tracker: Arc<T>,\n    ) -> Self {\n        let (metric_tx, mut metric_rx) = mpsc::channel::<MetricEvent>(METRIC_CHANNEL_CAPACITY);\n        let (retrain_tx, _) = broadcast::channel::<RetrainJob>(RETRAIN_CHANNEL_CAPACITY);\n\n        // In-memory state: per-model rolling window\n        let windows = Arc::new(RwLock::new(dashmap::DashMap::<String, MetricWindow>::new()));\n\n        // Clone tracker for the metric ingestion task\n        let tracker_for_metrics = Arc::clone(&tracker);\n\n        // Task 1: metric ingestion\n        let windows_clone = Arc::clone(&windows);\n        let metric_task = tokio::spawn(async move {\n            while let Some(evt) = metric_rx.recv().await {\n                counter!(\"metric_events_ingested\", 1, \"model\" => &evt.model_id);\n\n                // Log the metric to the experiment tracker\n                tracker_for_metrics.log_scalar(\n                    &format!(\"{}_latency_ms\", evt.model_id),\n                    evt.latency_ms,\n                    evt.ts as u64,\n                );\n                tracker_for_metrics.log_scalar(\n                    &format!(\"{}_throughput\", evt.model_id),\n                    evt.throughput,\n                    evt.ts as u64,\n                );\n                if let Some(acc) = evt.accuracy {\n                    tracker_for_metrics.log_scalar(\n                        &format!(\"{}_accuracy\", evt.model_id),\n                        acc,\n                        evt.ts as u64,\n                    );\n                }\n\n                let mut windows = windows_clone.write().await;\n                let window = windows\n                    .entry(evt.model_id.clone())\n                    .or_insert_with(MetricWindow::default);\n                window.push(evt);\n            }\n        });\n\n        // Task 2: periodic evaluation\n        let evaluation_task = {\n            let windows = Arc::clone(&windows);\n            let observers = observers\n                .into_iter()\n                .map(|o| (o.name(), o))\n                .collect::<Vec<_>>();\n            let mut retrain_tx = retrain_tx.clone();\n\n            tokio::spawn(async move {\n                let mut ticker = time::interval(DEFAULT_EVALUATION_INTERVAL);\n                loop {\n                    ticker.tick().await;\n                    let windows_guard = windows.read().await;\n\n                    for entry in windows_guard.iter() {\n                        let model = entry.key();\n                        let window = entry.value();\n\n                        if window.len() < 100 {\n                            // Not enough data yet\n                            continue;\n                        }\n\n                        let mut actions = Vec::with_capacity(observers.len());\n                        for (_, obs) in &observers {\n                            let a = obs.on_update(model, window);\n                            actions.push(a);\n                        }\n\n                        // Evaluate strategy\n                        if let Some(job) =\n                            strategy.evaluate(model, &actions, window).await\n                        {\n                            match retrain_tx.send(job.clone()) {\n                                Ok(_) => {\n                                    info!(\"Enqueued retrain job for model {}\", model);\n                                    counter!(\"retrain_jobs_enqueued\", 1, \"model\" => model);\n                                }\n                                Err(e) => {\n                                    error!(\"Failed to enqueue retrain job: {}\", e);\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            })\n        };\n\n        Self {\n            metric_sink: MetricSink { tx: metric_tx },\n            retrain_job_stream: RetrainJobStream {\n                rx: retrain_tx.subscribe(),\n            },\n            tasks: vec![metric_task, evaluation_task],\n            tracker,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn sink(&self) -> MetricSink {\n        self.metric_sink.clone()\n    }\n\n    pub fn retrain_jobs(&self) -> RetrainJobStream {\n        self.retrain_job_stream.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Get a reference to the experiment tracker.\n    pub fn tracker(&self) -> &Arc<T> {\n        &self.tracker\n    }\n\n    /// Gracefully stop tasks (await on JoinHandles)\n    pub async fn shutdown(self) {\n        for handle in self.tasks {\n            handle.abort(); // For brevity; in prod, send shutdown signal\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Legacy API for backward compatibility\nimpl MonitorEngine<DefaultTracker> {\n    /// Start the monitor engine using the legacy API.\n    ///\n    /// This maintains backward compatibility by creating a DefaultTracker\n    /// internally.\n    pub fn start(\n        observers: Vec<Box<dyn MetricObserver>>,\n        strategy: Arc<dyn RetrainStrategy>,\n    ) -> Self {\n        Self::start_with_default_tracker(observers, strategy, None)\n    }\n}\n\n// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Example integration test (can be toggled with `cargo test --lib`)\n// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use std::cell::RefCell;\n    use std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\n    /// Mock tracker for testing that records all operations without performing I/O.\n    struct MockTracker {\n        scalars: RefCell<Vec<(String, f64, u64)>>,\n        hyperparams: RefCell<Vec<(String, String)>>,\n        artifacts: RefCell<Vec<(PathBuf, String)>>,\n    }\n\n    impl MockTracker {\n        fn new() -> Self {\n            Self {\n                scalars: RefCell::new(Vec::new()),\n                hyperparams: RefCell::new(Vec::new()),\n                artifacts: RefCell::new(Vec::new()),\n            }\n        }\n\n        fn scalar_count(&self) -> usize {\n            self.scalars.borrow().len()\n        }\n    }\n\n    impl ExperimentTracker for MockTracker {\n        fn log_scalar(&self, metric_name: &str, value: f64, step: u64) {\n            self.scalars.borrow_mut().push((metric_name.to_string(), value, step));\n        }\n\n        fn log_hyperparameter(&self, param_name: &str, value: &str) {\n            self.hyperparams.borrow_mut().push((param_name.to_string(), value.to_string()));\n        }\n\n        fn upload_model_artifact(&self, local_path: &Path, remote_name: &str) -> Result<(), std::io::Error> {\n            self.artifacts.borrow_mut().push((local_path.to_path_buf(), remote_name.to_string()));\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Make MockTracker model.\nconst MAX_WINDOW_SIZE: usize = 5_000;\n/// Channel size for metric ingestion.\nconst METRIC_CHANNEL_CAPACITY: usize = 2048;\n/// Channel size for retraining job queue.\nconst RETRAIN_CHANNEL_CAPACITY: usize = 128;\n/// Default evaluation interval (how often we evaluate retraining strategies).\nconst DEFAULT_EVALUATION_INTERVAL: Duration = Duration::from_secs(60);\n/// Default experiment tracking endpoint\nconst DEFAULT_TRACKING_ENDPOINT: &str = \"http://localhost:5000\";\n\n/// Error types specific to Monitoring.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum MonitorError {\n    #[error(\"metrics channel closed\")]\n    ChannelClosed,\n    #[error(\"failed to send retraining job: {0}\")]\n    RetrainSend(String),\n    #[error(\"internal error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n}\n\n/// Public handle that can be cloned and used by inference workers to\n/// asynchronously submit new metric events.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct MetricSink {\n    tx: mpsc::Sender<MetricEvent>,\n}\n\nimpl MetricSink {\n    pub async fn submit(&self, evt: MetricEvent) -> Result<(), MonitorError> {\n        self.tx\n            .send(evt)\n            .await\n            .map_err(|_| MonitorError::ChannelClosed)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Public stream (subscriber) receiving retraining jobs that need handling\n/// downstream by Model-Ops components (e.g. a trainer dispatcher).\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct RetrainJobStream {\n    rx: broadcast::Receiver<RetrainJob>,\n}\n\nimpl RetrainJobStream {\n    pub async fn recv(&mut self) -> Result<RetrainJob, MonitorError> {\n        self.rx\n            .recv()\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| MonitorError::RetrainSend(e.to_string()))\n    }\n}\n\n/// Metric payload emitted by serving-layer components.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct MetricEvent {\n    pub model_id: String,\n    /// Unix-timestamp in milliseconds.\n    pub ts: u128,\n    /// End-to-end request latency observed by the client (ms).\n    pub latency_ms: f64,\n    /// Instantaneous throughput (# predictions / sec)\n    pub throughput: f64,\n    /// Running accuracy estimate (0.0 \u2013 1.0) if labels available.\n    pub accuracy: Option<f64>,\n}\n\nimpl MetricEvent {\n    pub fn now(\n        model_id: impl Into<String>,\n        latency_ms: f64,\n        throughput: f64,\n        accuracy: Option<f64>,\n    ) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            model_id: model_id.into(),\n            ts: SystemTime::now()\n                .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)\n                .expect(\"time went backwards\")\n                .as_millis(),\n            latency_ms,\n            throughput,\n            accuracy,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Rolling collection of metric events for a single model.\n#[derive(Debug, Default)]\nstruct MetricWindow {\n    /// Time-ordered ring-buffer\n    events: VecDeque<MetricEvent>,\n    /// Pre-aggregated stats for constant-time observers\n    latency_sum: f64,\n    throughput_sum: f64,\n    accuracy_sum: f64,\n    accuracy_cnt: usize,\n}\n\nimpl MetricWindow {\n    fn push(&mut self, evt: MetricEvent) {\n        if self.events.len() == MAX_WINDOW_SIZE {\n            if let Some(old) = self.events.pop_front() {\n                self.latency_sum -= old.latency_ms;\n                self.throughput_sum -= old.throughput;\n                if let Some(acc) = old.accuracy {\n                    self.accuracy_sum -= acc;\n                    self.accuracy_cnt -= 1;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        self.latency_sum += evt.latency_ms;\n        self.throughput_sum += evt.throughput;\n        if let Some(acc) = evt.accuracy {\n            self.accuracy_sum += acc;\n            self.accuracy_cnt += 1;\n        }\n\n        self.events.push_back(evt);\n    }\n\n    fn len(&self) -> usize {\n        self.events.len()\n    }\n\n    fn mean_latency(&self) -> f64 {\n        if self.events.is_empty() {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n        self.latency_sum / self.events.len() as f64\n    }\n\n    fn mean_throughput(&self) -> f64 {\n        if self.events.is_empty() {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n        self.throughput_sum / self.events.len() as f64\n    }\n\n    fn mean_accuracy(&self) -> Option<f64> {\n        if self.accuracy_cnt == 0 {\n            None\n        } else {\n            Some(self.accuracy_sum / self.accuracy_cnt as f64)\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn p99_latency(&self) -> f64 {\n        // naive percentile calc (production code may use histogram)\n        if self.events.is_empty() {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n        let mut latencies: Vec<_> = self.events.iter().map(|e| e.latency_ms).collect();\n        latencies.sort_by(|a, b| a.partial_cmp(b).unwrap());\n        let idx = ((latencies.len() as f64) * 0.99).ceil() as usize - 1;\n        latencies[idx]\n    }\n}\n\n/// What action an Observer suggests.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq)]\nenum MonitorAction {\n    Noop,\n    FlagRetrain,\n}\n\n/// Observer Pattern: notified of each model's aggregated metrics.\ntrait MetricObserver: Send + Sync {\n    /// Name (for logging/metrics)\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str;\n    /// Evaluate window; return action.\n    fn on_update(&self, model: &str, window: &MetricWindow) -> MonitorAction;\n}\n\n/// Observer that triggers retraining when P99 latency > threshold.\nstruct LatencySlaObserver {\n    /// milliseconds\n    threshold_ms: f64,\n}\n\nimpl LatencySlaObserver {\n    fn new(threshold_ms: f64) -> Self {\n        Self { threshold_ms }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MetricObserver for LatencySlaObserver {\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"latency_sla\"\n    }\n\n    fn on_update(&self, model: &str, window: &MetricWindow) -> MonitorAction {\n        let p99 = window.p99_latency();\n        gauge!(\"model.p99_latency\", p99, \"model\" => model);\n        if p99 > self.threshold_ms {\n            warn!(\n                \"Model {} P99 latency {:.2}ms above threshold {:.2}ms\",\n                model, p99, self.threshold_ms\n            );\n            return MonitorAction::FlagRetrain;\n        }\n        MonitorAction::Noop\n    }\n}\n\n/// Observer that detects accuracy drift below threshold.\nstruct AccuracyDriftObserver {\n    min_accuracy: f64,\n}\n\nimpl AccuracyDriftObserver {\n    fn new(min_accuracy: f64) -> Self {\n        Self { min_accuracy }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MetricObserver for AccuracyDriftObserver {\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"accuracy_drift\"\n    }\n\n    fn on_update(&self, model: &str, window: &MetricWindow) -> MonitorAction {\n        if let Some(acc) = window.mean_accuracy() {\n            gauge!(\"model.accuracy\", acc, \"model\" => model);\n            if acc < self.min_accuracy {\n                warn!(\n                    \"Model {} accuracy {:.4} below threshold {:.4}\",\n                    model, acc, self.min_accuracy\n                );\n                return MonitorAction::FlagRetrain;\n            }\n        }\n        MonitorAction::Noop\n    }\n}\n\n/// An internal representation of a retraining job request.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct RetrainJob {\n    pub model_id: String,\n    pub reason: String,\n    pub requested_at: u128,\n}\n\n/// Strategy Pattern: decides\u2014based on aggregated Observer signals\u2014if we should\n/// create a RetrainJob.\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\ntrait RetrainStrategy: Send + Sync {\n    /// Called periodically with aggregated observer actions\n    async fn evaluate(\n        &self,\n        model: &str,\n        actions: &[MonitorAction],\n        window: &MetricWindow,\n    ) -> Option<RetrainJob>;\n}\n\n/// Simple majority-vote strategy: if any FlagRetrain action is present,\n/// we create a job. Implements a debounce window to avoid spamming.\nstruct MajorityStrategy {\n    /// minimum time between two jobs for the same model\n    cooldown: Duration,\n    /// book-keeping of last job timestamps\n    last_job_ts: Arc<RwLock<dashmap::DashMap<String, u128>>>,\n}\n\nimpl MajorityStrategy {\n    fn new(cooldown: Duration) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            cooldown,\n            last_job_ts: Arc::new(RwLock::new(dashmap::DashMap::new())),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait::async_trait]\nimpl RetrainStrategy for MajorityStrategy {\n    async fn evaluate(\n        &self,\n        model: &str,\n        actions: &[MonitorAction],\n        _window: &MetricWindow,\n    ) -> Option<RetrainJob> {\n        if !actions.iter().any(|a| *a == MonitorAction::FlagRetrain) {\n            return None;\n        }\n\n        let now = SystemTime::now()\n            .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)\n            .unwrap()\n            .as_millis();\n\n        {\n            let m = self.last_job_ts.read().await;\n            if let Some(entry) = m.get(model) {\n                let last = *entry;\n                if now - last < self.cooldown.as_millis() {\n                    debug!(\"Skipping retrain for {model} due to cooldown\");\n                    return None;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        {\n            let mut m = self.last_job_ts.write().await;\n            m.insert(model.to_string(), now);\n        }\n\n        Some(RetrainJob {\n            model_id: model.to_string(),\n            reason: \"observer_trigger\".into(),\n            requested_at: now,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Create a DefaultTracker instance for experiment tracking.\n///\n/// This function creates the production tracker that wraps the internal\n/// `RawMetricClient`. It reads the endpoint from configuration or uses\n/// a default value.\npub fn create_experiment_tracker(endpoint: Option<&str>) -> DefaultTracker {\n    let tracking_endpoint = endpoint.unwrap_or(DEFAULT_TRACKING_ENDPOINT);\n    DefaultTracker::new(tracking_endpoint)\n}\n\n/// Central engine wiring together observers + strategy.\npub struct MonitorEngine<T: ExperimentTracker + Send + Sync + 'static> {\n    metric_sink: MetricSink,\n    retrain_job_stream: RetrainJobStream,\n    /// keep JoinHandles for graceful shutdown\n    tasks: Vec<JoinHandle<()>>,\n    /// Experiment tracker for logging metrics\n    tracker: Arc<T>,\n}\n\nimpl MonitorEngine<DefaultTracker> {\n    /// Start a new MonitorEngine with the DefaultTracker.\n    ///\n    /// This is the primary entry {\n    /// Start a new MonitorEngine with a custom tracker implementation.\n    ///\n    /// This allows for dependency injection of different tracker implementations,\n    /// including mocks for (metric_tx, mut metric_rx) = mpsc::channel::<MetricEvent>(METRIC_CHANNEL_CAPACITY);\n        let (retrain_tx, _) = broadcast::channel::<RetrainJob>(RETRAIN_CHANNEL_CAPACITY);\n\n        // In-memory tracker_for_metrics = Arc::clone(&tracker);\n\n        // Task 1: metric ingestion\n        let windows_clone = Arc::clone(&windows);\n        let metric_task = tokio::spawn(async move {\n            while let Some(evt) = metric_rx.recv().await {\n                counter!(\"metric_events_ingested\", 1, \"model\" => &evt.model_id);\n\n                // Log the metric to the experiment tracker\n                tracker_for_metrics.log_scalar(\n                    &format!(\"{}_latency_ms\", evt.model_id),\n                    evt.latency_ms,\n                    evt.ts as u64,\n      );\n                if let Some(acc) = evt.accuracy {\n                    tracker_for_metrics.log_scalar(\n                        &format!(\"{}_accuracy\", evt.model_id),\n                        acc,\n                        evt.ts as u64,\n                    );\n                }\n\n                let mut windows = windows_clone.write().await;\n                let window = windows\n                    .entry(evt.model_id.clone())\n                    .or_insert_with(MetricWindow::default);\n                window.push(evt);\n            }\n        });\n\n        // Task 2: periodic evaluation\n        let evaluation_task = {\n            let windows = Arc::clone(&windows);\n            let observers = observers\n                .into_iter()\n                .map(|o| (o.name(), o))\n                .collect::<Vec<_>>();\n            let mut retrain_tx = retrain_tx.clone();\n\n            tokio::spawn(async move {\n                let mut ticker = time::interval(DEFAULT_EVALUATION_INTERVAL);\n                loop {\n                    ticker.tick().await;\n                    let windows_guard = windows.read().await;\n\n                    for entry in windows_guard.iter() {\n                        let model = entry.key();\n                        let window = entry.value();\n\n                        if window.len() < 100 {\n                            // Not enough data yet\n                            continue;\n                        }\n\n                        let mut actions = Vec::with_capacity(observers.len());\n                        for (_, obs) in &observers {\n                            let a = obs.on_update(model, window);\n                            actions.push(a);\n                        }\n\n                        // Evaluate strategy\n                        if let Some(job) =\n                            strategy.evaluate(model, &actions, window).await\n                        {\n                            match retrain_tx.send(job.clone()) {\n                                Ok(_) => {\n                                    info!(\"Enqueued retrain job for model {}\", model);\n                                    counter!(\"retrain_jobs_enqueued\", 1, \"model\" => model);\n                                }\n                                Err(e) => {\n                                    error!(\"Failed to enqueue retrain job: {}\", e);\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            })\n        };\n\n        Self {\n            metric_sink: MetricSink { tx: metric_tx },\n            retrain_job_stream: RetrainJobStream {\n                rx: retrain_tx.subscribe(),\n            },\n            tasks: vec![metric_task, evaluation_task],\n            tracker,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn sink(&self) -> MetricSink {\n        self.metric_sink.clone()\n    }\n\n    pub fn &self.tracker\n    }\n\n    /// Gracefully stop tasks (await on JoinHandles)\n    pub async fn shutdown(self) {\n        for handle in self.tasks {\n            handle.abort(); // For brevity; in prod, send shutdown signal\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Legacy API for backward compatibility\nimpl MonitorEngine<DefaultTracker> {\n    /// Start the monitor engine using the legacy API.\n    ///\n                if d.magnitude > self.threshold {\n                    self.retrain_flag.store(true, Ordering::Relaxed);\n                    // Fire the notifier if present\n                    let _ = self.notifier.close();\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        pub async fn on_retrain(&mut self) -> Result<()> {\n            self.notifier.await.ok();\n            if self.retrain_flag.load(Ordering::Relaxed) {\n                Ok(())\n            } else {\n                Err(anyhow::anyhow!(\"retrain flag was never set\"))\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n Observed for ObservedDrift {\n        async fn on_event(&mut self, evt: Event) -> Result<()> {\n            self.emit(evt);\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Re-export stubs into parent assert_eq!(tracker.hyperparam_count(), 3);\n    assert_eq!(tracker.scalar_count(), 10); // 5 epochs * 2 metrics\n    assert_eq!(tracker.artifact_count(), 1);\n\n    // Verify specific metric values\n DefaultTracker Implementation\n\n```rust\n// File: /app/project/src/experiment_tracker.txt\n// Lines: 59-87\n\n/// Default implementation of `ExperimentTracker` that wraps `RawMetricClient`.\npub struct DefaultTracker {\n    client: RawMetricClient,\n}\n\nimpl DefaultTracker {\n    pub fn new(endpoint: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            client: RawMetricClient::new(endpoint),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl ExperimentTracker for DefaultTracker {\n    fn log_scalar(&self, metric_name: &str, value: f64, step: u64) {\n        self.client.log_scalar(metric_name, value, step);\n    }\n\n    fn log_hyperparameter(&self, param_name: &str, value: &str) {\n        self.client.log_hyperparameter(param_name, value);\n    }\n\n    fn upload_model_artifact(&self, local_path: &Path, remote_name: &str) -> Result<(), std::io::Error> {\n        self.client.upload_model_artifact(local_path, remote_name)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3. RawMetricClient (Made Crate-Private)\n\n```rust\n// File: /app/project/src/utils.txt\n// Lines: 380-425\n\n/// Low-level metric client for experiment tracking.\n///\n/// This struct is crate-private and should only be accessed through the\n/// `ExperimentTracker` trait abstraction in the `experiment_tracker` module.\npub(crate) struct RawMetricClient {\n    endpoint: String,\n}\n\nimpl RawMetricClient {\n    pub(crate) fn new(endpoint: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            endpoint: endpoint.into(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub(crate) fn log_scalar(&self, metric_name: &str, value: f64, step: u64) {\n        info!(\n            endpoint = %self.endpoint,\n            metric = %metric_name,\n            value = %value,\n            step = %step,\n            \"RawMetricClient: logged scalar\"\n        );\n    }\n\n    pub(crate) fn log_hyperparameter(&self, param_name: &str, value: &str) {\n        info!(\n            endpoint = %self.endpoint,\n            param = %param_name,\n            value = %value,\n            \"RawMetricClient: logged hyperparameter\"\n        );\n    }\n\n    pub(crate) fn upload_model_artifact(\n        &self,\n        local_path: &Path,\n        remote_name: &str,\n    ) -> Result<(), std::io::Error> {\n        info!(\n            endpoint = %self.endpoint,\n            local_path = %local_path.display(),\n            remote_name = %remote_name,\n            \"RawMetricClient: uploaded model artifact\"\n        );\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 4.     }\n    }\n\n    pub fn scalar_count(&self) -> usize { self.scalars.borrow().len() }\n    pub fn hyperparam_count(&self) -> usize { self.hyperparams.borrow().len() }\n    pub fn      self.artifacts.borrow_mut().push((local_path.to_path_buf(), remote_name.to_string()));\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Architectural Pattern: Trait-Based Abstraction (Dependency Inversion)\n\nThe refactoring implements the **Dependency Inversion Principle (DIP)** from SOLID principles, specifically using Rust's trait system for abstraction:\n\n1. **High-level modules** (`module_34.txt`, `module_62.txt`, `module_7.txt`) depend on the abstract `ExperimentTracker` trait, not the concrete `RawMetricClient`.\n\n2. **Low-level modules** (`RawMetricClient`) are wrapped by `DefaultTracker`, which implements the trait.\n\n3. **Both depend on abstractions** - the `ExperimentTracker` trait serves as the contract between them.\n\n### Benefits of This Architecture\n\n1. **Testability**: The `MockTracker` allows unit testing without I/O operations or network calls.\n\n2. **Flexibility**: New tracking backends can be added by implementing `ExperimentTracker` without modifying existing code.\n\n3. **Encapsulation**: `RawMetricClient` is now `pub(crate)`, preventing direct usage from outside the crate.\n\n4. **Type Safety**: Generic functions with `<T: ExperimentTracker>` provide compile-time verification.\n\n### Component Interactions\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: Successfully decoupled experiment tracking logic using Rust's trait-based abstraction pattern\n- **Key components**:\n  - `ExperimentTracker` trait - core abstraction\n  - `DefaultTracker` - production implementation\n  - `RawMetricClient` - encapsulated low-level client\n  - `MockTracker` - test implementation\n- **Architectural pattern**: Dependency (Dependency Inversion)\n\nThe refactoring implements the **Dependency Inversion Principle (DIP)** from SOLID principles, specifically using Rust's trait system for abstraction:\n\n1. **High-level modules** (`module_34.txt`, `module_62.txt`, `module_7.txt`) depend on the abstract `ExperimentTracker` trait, not the concrete `RawMetricClient`.\n\n2. **Low-level modules** (`RawMetricClient`) are wrapped by `DefaultTracker`, which implements the trait.\n\n3. **Both depend on abstractions** - the `ExperimentTracker` trait serves as the contract between them.\n\n### Benefits of This Architecture\n\n1. **Testability**: The `MockTracker` allows unit testing without I/O operations or network calls.\n\n2. **Flexibility**: New tracking backends can be added by implementing `ExperimentTracker` without modifying existing code.\n\n3. **Encapsulation**: `RawMetricClient` is now `pub(crate)`, preventing direct usage from outside the crate.\n\n4. **Type Safety**: Generic functions with `<T: ExperimentTracker>` provide compile-time verification.\n\n### Component ```rust
//! Experiment Tracking Abstraction Layer
//! =====================================
//!
//! This module provides a trait-based abstraction for experiment tracking,
//! decoupling the core ML training and hyperparameter tuning logic from
//! concrete tracking implementations.
//!
//! # Design Rationale
//!
//! The `ExperimentTracker` trait allows for:
//! - Easy swapping of tracking backends (MLflow, W&B, local files, etc.)
//! - Mock implementations for testing without I/O
//! - Clean separation of concerns
//!
//! # Usage
//!
//! Functions that need to log metrics should accept a generic parameter
//! bounded by `ExperimentTracker`:
//!
//! ```rust
//! fn train_model<T: ExperimentTracker>(tracker: &T, ...) {
//!     tracker.log_scalar("loss", 0.5, 1);
//!     tracker.log_hyperparameter("learning_rate", "0.001");
//! }
//! ```

use std::path::Path;

use crate::RawMetricClient;

/// Trait abstracting experiment tracking operations.
///
/// Implementors of this trait can log metrics, hyperparameters, and artifacts
/// to various backends (local files, MLflow, cloud services, etc.).
pub trait ExperimentTracker: Send + Sync {
    /// Log a scalar metric value at a given training step.
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `metric_name` - Name of the metric (e.g., "loss", "accuracy")
    /// * `value` - The scalar value to log
    /// * `step` - The training step or epoch number
    fn log_scalar(&self, metric_name: &str, value: f64, step: u64);

    /// Log a hyperparameter configuration.
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `param_name` - Name of the hyperparameter (e.g., "learning_rate")
    /// * `value` - String representation of the hyperparameter value
    fn log_hyperparameter(&self, param_name: &str, value: &str);

    /// Upload a model artifact to the tra
... (truncated)
3. WRITE /tmp/refactoring_output/src/experiment_tracker.txt
```rust
//! Experiment Tracking Abstraction Layer
//! =====================================
//!
//! This module provides a trait-based abstraction for experiment tracking,
//! decoupling the core ML training and hyperparameter tuning logic from
//! concrete tracking implementations.
//!
//! # Design Rationale
//!
//! The `ExperimentTracker` trait allows for:
//! - Easy swapping of tracking backends (MLflow, W&B, local files, etc.)
//! - Mock implementations for testing without I/O
//! - Clean separation of concerns
//!
//! # Usage
//!
//! Functions that need to log metrics should accept a generic parameter
//! bounded by `ExperimentTracker`:
//!
//! ```rust
//! fn train_model<T: ExperimentTracker>(tracker: &T, ...) {
//!     tracker.log_scalar("loss", 0.5, 1);
//!     tracker.log_hyperparameter("learning_rate", "0.001");
//! }
//! ```

use std::path::Path;

use crate::RawMetricClient;

/// Trait abstracting experiment tracking operations.
///
/// Implementors of this trait can log metrics, hyperparameters, and artifacts
/// to various backends (local files, MLflow, cloud services, etc.).
pub trait ExperimentTracker: Send + Sync {
    /// Log a scalar metric value at a given training step.
    ///

/// VisuTility's generic error type for utility-layer operations.
///
/// We prefer using [`anyhow::Error`] at the top-level application
/// boundary to allow for heterogeneous sources, but within the
/// utility layer we capture the most common failure categories so that
/// callers can still pattern-match when they need to.
#[derive(Debug, Error)]
pub enum UtilError {
    #[error("I/O error: {0}")]
    Io(#[from] std::io::Error),

    #[error("serialization error: {0}")]
    Serde(#[from] serde_json::Error),

    #[error("configuration not found at path `{0}`")]
    ConfigNotFound(PathBuf),

    #[error("task failed: {0}")]
    TaskFailed(String),
}

# Solution: rust_ml_computer_vision_expert_054_cross_file_refactoring_expert_01

## Code Evidence

### 1. New ExperimentTracker Trait Definition

```rust
// File: /app/project/src/experiment_tracker.txt
// Lines: 26-57

use std::path::Path;

use crate::RawMetricClient;

/// Trait abstracting experiment tracking operations.
///
/// Implementors of this trait can log metrics, hyperparameters, and artifacts
/// to various backends (local files, MLflow, cloud services, etc.).
pub trait ExperimentTracker: Send + Sync {
    /// Log a scalar metric value at a given training step.
    fn log_scalar(&self, metric_name: &str, value: f64, step: u64);

    /// Log a hyperparameter configuration.
    fn log_hyperparameter(&self, param_name: &str, value: &str);

    /// Upload a model artifact to the tracking server.
    fn upload_model_artifact(&self, local_path: &Path, remote_name: &str) -> Result<(), std::io::Error>;
}
```
